 ;CODE MEMORY: (0x00000000-0x0000FFFF) 
 ;DATA MEMORY: (0x00010000-0x0001FFFF) 

 org 0000 

 mfc0 $16, $13
 beq $16, $0, _reset

 exception_handler: 
	mfc0 $16, $12
	mfc0 $17, $13
	mfc0 $19, $14
	mfc0 $20, $15
	sw $16, 0($29)
	sw $17, 4($29)
	sw $19, 8($29)
	sw $20, 12($29)
	addi $19, $19, 4
	mtc0 $19, $14
	mfc0 $21, $12
	addi $21, $21, 65533
	ori $21, $21, 1
	mtc0 $21, $12
	cop0 4
	jr $19

 _reset: 
	xor $0, $0, $0
	xor $1, $1, $1
